Jiangyin 71

A Dispute over Sandy Land: The Sandy Land Bureau of Jiangyin received a report from Zhu Tingyan, a resident of the county, and others, alleging that Zhu Tingyan and others from Shazhou had gathered people to cross the border and build embankment walls and requested an investigation. The Sandy Land Bureau immediately transferred the case to the county for investigation. Magistrate Li then issued a warrant to the political police Sun Pei to arrest Zhu Tingyan. On the afternoon of the 8th, the agents of the plaintiffs Zhu Tinghua, Qian Yulin, and Zhu Tingqiu were summoned for questioning. Zhu Tingyan claimed that he was not building the embankment wall across the border, but that the Fulai Company had recruited more than a thousand mud workers, given them certificates of pickets, and enclosed the fields according to the shares. Qian Yulin and others said that the plaintiffs had reported old cases and had already been approved by the Sandy Land Bureau to determine property rights and could build the embankment. Zhu Tingyan used the excuse of pickets, deliberately violated the law, infringed on rights, crossed the border, rushed to build the embankment, and fabricated accusations to frame people. Whether there is a property right and whether the embankment was built in Dong are documented in the files of the Sandy Land Bureau. After the interrogation by Yang, the judge, it was found that the case involved a complicated dispute over sandy land. Zhu Tingyan was allowed to post bail pending trial.

Robbers Attempted an Abortive Robbery in Sanguan Township: At about 1 a.m. yesterday (the 8th), dozens of robbers, armed and speaking with accents from north of the Yangtze River, suddenly surrounded Sanguan Township outside the East Gate on all sides. When they arrived at Dongxiang Gate, they fired two shots first. The guards at the Second Public Security Substation heard the alarm and returned fire. The security team also heard the sound and gathered to rush to the scene. The police and security team resisted the robbers for about half an hour, and the robbers retreated. When the two sides exchanged fire, gunshots were also faintly heard in the city. After the robbers retreated, they went to Huangjiawan and robbed the home of Huang Chunlin, losing hundreds of yuan. They also went to the homes of Zhou Bingrong in Zhoujiagu and Hu Shunsheng in Hu Sanqiao to ask for loans of silver dollars. The merchants and residents of Sanguan Temple were frightened by this incident and took their men and women to flee. The patrol officer Fan Yu is now making every effort to prevent it and has reported it to the General Bureau for handling.

Zhenjiang 72

The Department of Agriculture Orders the Clearing of Agricultural and Forestry Funds: The Department of Agriculture and Mines of Jiangsu Province believes that the counties have been collecting agricultural and forestry funds, but usually use the excuse of insufficient revenue and expenditure to fail to issue them on time and arbitrarily divert them for other uses. Now, the financial bureaus of Jiangpu, Yiwei, and other counties are

ordered to be abolished. The forest farms in various counties have repeatedly telegraphed that the heads of the financial bureaus have many cases of arrears, which is a very inappropriate situation. Therefore, it ordered the governments of Jiangpu, Yiwei, Su, Peixian, Chongming, Guanyun, Qidong, Yi County, Gan, Huaiyin, Yangzhong, Gangshan, Donghai, Xiaoxian, Suining, Pixian, Yu Shan, and other counties to instruct the heads of the financial bureaus of each county to allocate the agricultural and forestry funds collected during their tenure in full and to instruct them to notify the directors of the county farms in accordance with the No. 262 circular of the department to join the accounting. If there are any diversions or arrears, they must be cleared within a limited time and reported to the county farm directors for verification; otherwise, they will be held responsible for withholding and not allowed to leave the county.

Yangzhou 73

The Water Level of the Huai Canal Rises Sharply: The water level of the Huai Canal basin has risen sharply due to peach blossoms. According to reports from various sources by the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Office, the water level of the Qingjiang Canal has risen by 10.13 meters in one day, the water level of the Huai River in Bengbu has risen by 15.08 meters in two days, the water level from Gaoyou to the wharf has risen to 8.4 feet above the mark in five days, and the water level of the Shaobo Sangu Canal Gate has risen to 11.4 feet above the mark in six days, all of which are rare in the peach blossom flood and still have a tendency to continue to rise. It is said that this is due to the small dams returning to the Yangtze River being opened less and the river surface not being emptied in advance, and also due to heavy rain. If the autumn flood rises again, the thin canal embankment on the line is not reliable.

The Murderer Is Sentenced to Imprisonment and Refuses to Accept: Hu Hongsheng, the murderer who opened a jade shop and beat the apprentice Zhu Dajiu to death, was arrested after his corpse father Qilin sued the county last year. He has now been sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment by Cheng, the judge of Guan. Unexpectedly, Hu declared that he was not convinced and requested an appeal, and begged to have his shackles removed. The court granted his request and, in addition to ordering him to withdraw his application for appeal, signed the words "remove shackles" on the return warrant and sent him to prison.

Gao Fuqing's House Was Burned Down by Bandits: Gao Fuqing, of Ma Bailing Di, Yaojiadianqian, had recently moved his family to the city to avoid bandits who were demanding money. Bandits Riot in Guanyintang: In Guanyintang, Jinsha District, a large group of bandits rioted on the 7th. Reporting Grain Merchants for Hoarding and Profiteering: The grain shortage in Tong County has caused the price per stone to rise to 25 yuan and 30 cents. After investigation, it was confirmed that they would be ordered to sell it at a flat price.

Qianzhen Town Was Looted by Bandits: At 2 a.m. on the 8th, 400 bandits suddenly arrived in Qiantao Town, Nantong. They first surrounded the Public Security Bureau, looted all the weapons and ammunition, and set fire to the bureau. Then they robbed shops and residents, and no one in the city was spared. Many policemen were injured. At dawn, the bandit leader led the team to flee in the direction of Erjing. The town is a prosperous area in the east, and this looting caused extremely large losses. The national army and provincial police team stationed in the city have rushed to suppress the bandits.

Counter-Revolutionaries in Tongcheng Cause Trouble: At 8 p.m. on the 7th, 20 to 30 counter-revolutionaries in Tongcheng Xidajie Zhongshi suddenly distributed leaflets and shouted slogans, causing trouble in the vicinity for more than ten minutes. At the same time, false alarms arose in all directions. By the time the military and police arrived, the counter-revolutionaries had dispersed.

The Provincial Electrical Industry Holds a Meeting in Nantong: The Jiangsu Provincial Electrical Industry is scheduled to hold a joint meeting at the Nantong Club on the 10th. Representatives from various counties have come to Nantong one after another.

Rugao 76

A Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits in Dingzhuang: On the evening of the 2nd, the military and political agencies of Rugao sent provincial police to lead the first platoon of the city's security regiment to Laohuzhuang in Motou District to search and suppress bandits. At 6 a.m. the next day, they encountered more than 5,000 bandits in Dingzhuang, 20 miles from Laohuzhuang. After three hours of fighting, the bandits were defeated and retreated. In this battle, more than 80 bandits were killed and countless bandits were injured. Four bandits were captured alive, and four of them were beheaded on the spot and sent to the county for public display. When the Fourth Provincial Police Squadron was pursuing the bandits, it also captured three bandit suspects and sent them to the county for interrogation. During the fierce battle, the bandits set fire to the houses west of the river in Laohuzhuang and the Zhang surname wood business to create a false impression of strength, causing huge losses. It is now heard that the county government intends to allocate funds to build a fortress in Laohuzhuang, a major town in the south of the county, to defend it.

A Group of Bandits Gather in Jia Cai Village: At about 5 a.m. on the 5th, more than 500 bandits gathered in Jia Cai Village, Motou District, with the intention of rioting. The garrison stationed there learned of this and took precautions, and immediately telegraphed the county government and the Defense Committee to request troops to suppress the bandits. Commander Li Changjiang then personally led the Fourth Provincial Police Squadron, the Liu Ruiming Department, the Zhao Qisheng Department of the Second Machine Gun Team, and a squad from the Public Security Bureau's Box Team, along with the Second County Police Squadron, to suppress the bandits.

Jiaxing 77

Location of District Offices: The Jiaxing Autonomous Region has been divided into seven districts by the county government after repeatedly convening representatives of the county's villages and neighborhoods. The division has been approved by the Department of Civil Affairs, and the provincial committee has appointed Shang Baoshan and six others as district chiefs. It is now learned that the county government has also ordered the heads of the public security bureaus of each district to report the locations of the district offices. Most of the heads of the public security bureaus have reported the location of the bureau to the county. The county government seems to agree with this.

Progress in Holding Flat-Price Grain Sales: Jiaxing has organized a committee to hold flat-price grain sales and has stipulated that 15,000 yuan will be allocated to cover losses. However, the investigation of poor households is the most troublesome and difficult to do fairly. The committee has now decided to entrust the investigation of poor households to the village and neighborhood committees and the autonomous instructors of each district for the sake of accuracy. Therefore, the county magistrate issued orders to the autonomous instructors of each district and the village and neighborhood committees yesterday, asking them to submit a list of poor households in their territory by the 10th of the month for distribution.

Businesses Jointly Request Exemption from Demolition: The Xuangong Bridge outside the East Gate of Jiaxing has been rebuilt as a cement bridge, and the houses on both sides have also been demolished separately. Now, the Construction Bureau of the county government suddenly intends to redraw the street to build sidewalks on both sides of the bridge, ordering the houses on both sides to be moved back another 14 feet and to be demolished by the end of May. Thirty-three businesses, including Shengchang, Yian, and Yuchang, have jointly petitioned the provincial and county authorities, requesting them to sympathize with the difficulties of the merchants, consider the livelihood of the people, and temporarily exempt them from execution to maintain the commercial market.

Hangzhou 78

Organization of Public Bonds to be Drawn by Lot on Schedule: The Zhejiang Department of Finance has scheduled the eighth redemption of the old public bonds in the province on the afternoon of the 15th and especially asked various agencies to send personnel to the venue to observe in order to show great faith.

Invention of Supermagnetic Telephone: After inventing the supermagnetic telephone, Chen Shaolin, an engineer from Zhejiang, continued to invent a long-distance telephone bridging method. Yesterday, Chen submitted a presentation to the Construction Department asking them to send personnel to conduct an experiment to prove its effectiveness so that it could be submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to apply for a patent for 15 years.

County Magistrates Take Office Yesterday: Ten of the Zhejiang province's third term of county magistrates have been appointed, including Zhao Tianhe, Zhou Lianglinze, etc., and three have been appointed for long-term training, including Xu Qihui, etc. Yesterday (the 9th) afternoon, Chairman Zhang issued certificates in the auditorium of the provincial government, and Director Zhu of the Civil Affairs Department gave a speech.

Fake Director Has Been Escorted Back to Justice: After the Provincial Government secretly ordered the Provincial Public Security Bureau to arrest thirty-seven people, including the fake Deputy Director of the Zhejiang Preparatory Office of the Central Army Teaching Regiment, the fugitive fake Director Xu Yuanchun dared to go to the Civil Affairs Department yesterday afternoon to see the Second Section Chief. Section Chief Jiang immediately notified Zhang Ganchen, the section chief of the First Section of the Security Office, and secretly ordered the Patrol Brigade to arrest him. According to his confession, he was appointed by Zhang Benxing Zhongchaojin in the capital. Xu has now been transferred to the military law office.

Ningbo 79

Two Kidnappings: Wang Jinxian and Wang Jinshan, two farmers from Chuanjialu in Dongxiang, Yuyao, loaded fir firewood to sell in Yao City the day before. When their boat reached Hengshan, two robber boats suddenly came and more than twenty bandits looted them and kidnapped Jinxian and Jinshan and headed west. Before leaving, the bandits said that they would contact them for the ransom in Baisha Bay.

Also, Xu Zhengyun, a farmer from Zhangyang Village, Shanyuan District, Fenghua, was stingy and had a lot of savings. Unexpectedly, yesterday evening, Huang, a former long-term worker who had been dismissed, led more than ten bandits to kidnap Xu Zhengyun and demanded 5,000 yuan.

Letters Received

Letter from the Military Law Office of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force: 80

Dear Sir/Madam,

I have just read a news item in your newspaper on May 5 about a telegram from Nanjing stating that Fang Zhenwu had moved to Gulou Hospital for medical treatment and that the General Headquarters had sent personnel to take care of him. After investigation, the statement is not true. I am writing to inform you of this and hope that you will make corrections. Sincerely, Military Law Office of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force.

Letter from the Jiading County Construction Bureau: 81

I recently read a news item in the Local Communications column of your newspaper on May 9 entitled "Reasons for the Slow Installation of Long-Distance Telephones in Ji County," which does not conform to the facts. After investigation, the installation of long-distance telephones in our county has already begun. Within two months, all districts in the county will be able to make calls. What your newspaper reported is probably based on false rumors. I am writing to inform you of this and request that you make corrections. I will be very grateful. Sincerely, Jiading County Construction Bureau, May 9, 1920.

Yesterday's Activities 82

Commemorating the National Humiliation of May 9th

Yesterday (the 9th) was the anniversary of the National Humiliation Day in the fourth year of the Republic of China when Japanese imperialism coerced the false Beijing government into signing the Twenty-One Demands. The Preparatory Committee for the May Revolution Commemoration Day in this city specially held a grand meeting of all sectors to commemorate the National Humiliation of May 9th at the Penglai Grand Theater at 9 a.m. yesterday. More than 800 representatives from various agencies, groups, and schools attended. Chairman Chen Dezheng reported on the significance of the commemoration and the efforts that all sectors should make to commemorate the National Humiliation. Then, Li Ruzhang, Li Yongxiang, Fu Depei, and others gave speeches. After shouting slogans, the Revolutionary Drama Society of the First District Party Department performed the play "Awakened." The Ministry of Health Convenes 83

The Third Cholera Prevention Meeting in Shanghai

Held at the Municipal Government's Recreation Club at 3 p.m. on the 9th

The Ministry of Health believes that the annual cholera epidemic in Shanghai has a significant impact on China's foreign trade and international reputation. It has convened two prevention meetings in Shanghai. Now that summer is approaching and the work needs to be stepped up, a third meeting was specially convened at the Municipal Government's Recreation Club at 3 p.m. yesterday, inviting relevant parties. Those who attended the meeting included Liu Ruiheng, Minister of Health, Hu Hongji, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, Davis, Director of the Health Department of the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, Zhu Erdian, Deputy Director, Futianya, Director of the French Concession Engineering Bureau, Yan Fuqing, Director of the Red Cross General Hospital, Hu Xuanpeng, Director of the Health Department of the Ministry of Railways, Cai Hong, Director of the Ministry of Health, Jin Baoshan, Technical Supervisor Wu Liande, Cheng Muyi, Director of the Health Experimental Institute, etc., as well as Dr. Ittiti, Director of the Far East Intelligence Bureau in Singapore, and Dr. Parker, who attended to offer their opinions. It is heard that the Municipal Health Bureau has decided to spend 10,000 yuan, the Public Concession Engineering Bureau will spend 5,000 taels, the French Concession Engineering Bureau will spend 12,000 taels, and the Ministry of Health will subsidize 10,000 yuan, and will send specialized technical personnel to cooperate in the work to ensure that the cholera epidemic will no longer be seen in Shanghai.

Delegates 84

to the Labor Conference Set Sail Yesterday

The World Labor Conference is scheduled to be held in Geneva, Italy on June 10. China is also a member of the conference and is attending the meeting. The conference has sent a telegram urging the dispatch of representatives to attend the meeting. The Central Government has specially appointed Zhu Shikang and Ms. He Xiulan and three others as official representatives. After Zhu and others arrived in Shanghai, they initially planned to take a European ship to France and then transfer to Italy. However, due to the urgency of the meeting, there was only one month left before the opening. If they took a European ship, there would not be enough time to attend the meeting. Therefore, they changed their sea route to go from the Pacific Ocean to the United States and then cross the Atlantic Ocean to Geneva, which would allow them to arrive around June 5th or 6th. Therefore, at 9 a.m. yesterday, the three representatives purchased tickets for the President Madison of the Dollar Steamship Company and boarded the ship at the New Customs Wharf. They departed from the country that day.

Chen Zongcheng, the secretary of the International Labor Bureau, a native of Guangdong, has returned to China from Geneva to take office as the director of the International Labor Branch. He arrived in Shanghai at noon on the 9th of this month aboard the French postal ship GENERALMETZINGE accompanied by his family. The ship docked at the China Merchants Bureau's Zhongzhan Wharf. Zhao Zhizhi, director of the China Seamen's Industrial Federation, Lin Youneng, Miao Shuizhang, Qiu Yaokuan, and He Zhenhuan, a standing member of the Seamen's Shanghai Branch, led hundreds of staff and workers, as well as Wang Renlin, the labor representative to the 12th International Labor Conference, to welcome him at the ship. Chen Zongcheng met them in the ship's dining room and shook hands with them one by one as a courtesy. He then disembarked and gave a brief speech to the seamen and expressed his gratitude. Then he took his family by car to Cangzhou Villa on Yuyuan Road. It is heard that Chen will stay here and go to Beijing during the day to take office.

Traveling East on the Shanghai Maru on the Fourteenth of This Month

In addition, his personality is extremely pleasing to China, and his relationship with the National Government is particularly good. This may also be an important reason for his promotion to minister. The Naval Reorganization Office Will Close Today 95

The Naval Reorganization Office at Gaochang Temple was established in Shanghai in May of last year upon order, and eleven people, including Yang Shuzhuang, Chen Shaokuan, Ling Xiao, Zhang Qun, Huang Xuyu, Chen Jiliang, Wang Lie, Zeng Yiding, and Liu Chuanshou, were appointed as members. It has been almost a year. However, our country's navy is very different from the army. Its strength is weak, and it is not enough to speak of national defense. Therefore, although it is called reorganization, in reality, it is just a little inspection and rectification, and there is no so-called reorganization or dismissal. Moreover, the members hold multiple positions and are often out. Since the Ling and Wang members returned to the Northeast, the routine weekly reorganization committee has not been able to be held as usual. The Central Reorganization Committee has therefore instructed the office to immediately abolish it. After receiving the order, the office decided to complete the closure today (the 10th). In the future, the name of the Naval Headquarters will still be used, and all personnel of the office will still be placed in the headquarters.

Upriver 96

British Ships Stop Using Chinese River Pilots

An Unfortunate Piece of News for the Lives of Chinese People

The negotiations between British ships and Chinese river pilots for upriver sailing have broken down. Previously, due to the increasing cost of living, the river pilots requested a raise in salary. The foreign ships then went on strike to deal with the situation. Later, American and Japanese shipping companies negotiated with the river pilots due to business relations and agreed to varying degrees of pay increases. Therefore, American and Japanese upriver ships resumed their routes within the past month, as reported in this newspaper. British companies, such as Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire, were the most vehement opponents of the pay increase. Later, they were forced by the resumption of routes by Chinese, Japanese, and American ships to seriously consider the impact on their business. They negotiated with the river pilots on the issue of pay increases. After half a month, the British were extremely unwilling to compromise, and there was no opportunity for the labor and management sides to reach an agreement. According to a recent telegram from Yichang, the negotiations have broken down, and the British have indicated that they will temporarily not use Chinese river pilots.

Foreigners Are Cleverly Sailing Ships: Swire has a total of eight ships sailing upstream, and Jardine Matheson also has three. Some ships have been suspended in Shanghai for two months, and some for one month. Recently, because the river water between Yichang and Chongqing has risen greatly, large ships of more than 1,000 tons can pass through. The Sichuan cotton yarn purchasers have telegraphed Shanghai to rush to load and go to Chongqing. China Merchants, Nissin, and Czech companies have all sent large amounts of cargo. Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson are unwilling to give up this great business opportunity. Therefore, the seven large upstream ships in Shanghai have also successively transported yarn to Chongqing since the 4th of this month. However, the Yichang-Chongqing route cannot be sailed without Chinese river pilots. Since the British companies refused the river pilots' demands, they decided that the British shipowners would drive the ships themselves. They first went to Yichang to pick up the goods. On one hand, they secretly hired a Chinese person who was familiar with the Sichuan river routes at a good price to guide the foreign drivers on the first ship. The other ships followed along. Therefore, the British ships did not hire river pilots and were actually able to operate. The Wanxian, Wantong, and Wanliu wheels, which exported the previous and past days, all followed this method.

Movements of Foreign Warships Stationed in Shanghai 99

American Fleet Goes to the Bohai Sea: Two squadrons of American destroyers stationed in Shanghai had previously sent one squadron to Qingdao in early May. The six ships staying in Shanghai, including Nos. 30, 31, 32, 33, 34, and 35, have received orders from the Naval Admiral stationed in Shanghai after replenishing their military supplies, adding food, and coal, and have also sailed to Bohai Bay yesterday.

Japanese Navy Inspects the Japanese First Overseas Dispatch Team: The Japanese First Overseas Dispatch Team stationed in Shanghai is currently being inspected by Colonel Yamanouchi Toyonaka, a military attaché sent by the Japanese Emperor on the Nagasaki Maru wheel to China for inspection and consolation. After Yamanouchi arrived in Shanghai, he stayed at the Toyo Hotel. The Japanese Naval Commander stationed in Shanghai, Minai, Commander Shibata, and Consul Miura all went to welcome him. On the previous two days, Military Attaché Yamanouchi inspected the Japanese warships staying in Shanghai, including Hirato, Saga, Sumida, Urakaze, Futami, and Atami, and conveyed the Emperor's message of consolation. It was also decided that at 10:00 a.m. today, Commander Minai would mobilize 1,000 Japanese marines stationed in Shanghai at the New Park on Jiangwan Road and other places to prepare for Yamanouchi's inspection and hold a military parade. After inspecting Shanghai, Yamanouchi will go to Yichang and Changsha to inspect the upstream ships, and then return to Shanghai to Qingdao to console the ships of the Second Overseas Dispatch Team.

Problem of Rising Yangtze River Ferry Ticket Prices 100

Since the rise in gold prices, all ferry tickets have taken the opportunity to increase in price. On the Yangtze River route, Butterfield & Swire first proposed to increase the original amount by 10%. For example, the price from Shanghai to Hankou, which was originally 66 yuan, would increase to 72 yuan. Later, Taikoo, China Merchants, etc. did not agree, so this matter was not implemented. Now Nissin Company has also proposed the idea of ​​appropriately increasing ticket prices, and also proposes that future round-trip tickets, which are charged at 70%, should be changed to 100%. Currently, various shipping companies are discussing this. Recently, Yangtze River passenger tickets have become a situation where each company sets its own price because the six companies cannot agree. For example, the first-class passenger fare from Shanghai to Hankou on foreign ships is 66 yuan, while China Merchants Bureau ships only charge 52 yuan, so there is a big difference.

Silk Cocoon Association 101

Telegram Requesting Postponement of Cocoon Donation Security Fee

Huang Jinzhin, Chairman of the Jiangzhewan Silk Cocoon General Office, telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government yesterday: "Zhang, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, recently learned that the 308th Provincial Affairs Conference of the Zhejiang Provincial Government resolved to collect a security fee of 10% from this year's cocoon donation. The merchants were shocked to hear this. The Zhejiang Province's original cocoon donation is already heavily burdened. The merchants have fulfilled their tax obligations, and the government should have security responsibilities. Now, a new name has been established and a surcharge has been added. At a time when silk prices have fallen sharply and the silk cocoon industry is extremely difficult, it is really unable to bear it. It is requested that your general office submit a request to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to cancel the surcharge to stabilize the cocoon industry. Based on this, the Zhejiang Province's cocoon donation is already about 50% of the tax in addition to the regular tax of 8 yuan. Various surcharges have been added for a long time without being removed. The merchant's power is dwindling and they are already struggling to bear it. In the government's collection of donations and taxes, it should fulfill its responsibility to protect commerce, not to increase the security fee under the cocoon donation. In recent years, the cost of cocoons has been high and the price of silk has been low, resulting in years of losses and a difficult situation. If an exceptional surcharge is added to raw silk materials, it is tantamount to accelerating its demise. Jiahu is a more prosperous area for silk cocoons and should maintain its vitality to relieve cocoon production. According to the previous situation, it is no wonder that they are panic-stricken. It is specially telegraphed to humbly request the president to consider that the cocoon tax is heavy and to strive for the benefit of the hometown, and to postpone the implementation of the 10% security fee added to the cocoon donation to sympathize with farmers and merchants and relieve the people's power. I am extremely eager to await orders and hope for approval and instructions, which is a public convenience."

Ministry of Communications 104

The International Radio Station Will Be Powered by Zhabei

The Public Utilities Bureau Approved the Handling

The preparatory office of the International Communications Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications is constructing the International Wireless Radio Station in front of the Jinwang Temple in Shuangshier Tu, Zhenru. The radio station requires a large amount of power for its transmitting station, reaching 500 kilowatts. The local Zhenru Electric Company is small in scale and sells electricity from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, so it is unable to supply it directly and voluntarily waives this business right. The office then negotiated with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to undertake it and agreed to advance the company 50,000 yuan for installation and construction costs, which will be deducted from the electricity bill each month in the future. The company did not dare to specialize because the matter was outside the scope of the power supply business area and requested the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau to review and instruct. It is now known that the bureau has approved its temporary power supply, but in the future

If there is another registered electrical company in the area, all the company's power supply equipment in the area will be taken back at a price, and it will be ordered to submit the contract concluded with the radio station for filing.

Relief Rice from Anhui Province Shipped 105

A Thousand Stones Shipped Out Yesterday

This year, there is a great famine in central Anhui. The provincial government has specially sent Jin Xi and others to Shanghai to purchase foreign rice and transport it to Anqing and other ports to open a cheap business. The first batch of 3,000 bags has been processed and the Sanbei Company has been negotiated to collect half the water feet and transport it to Anqing. One thousand stones were shipped out yesterday, and the rest will be transported next week. It is reported that the rice is sold for only ten yuan per stone in Anhui.

Spring Cocoons from Zhejiang Province Are on the Market 106

The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau Adds Cars

The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway transports this year's spring cocoons from various parts of Zhejiang Province. The Huitong Transport Company continues to contract with the Railway Bureau to continue to transport them. Yuhang was the earliest to open the scales and buy them. The cocoon price is 50 yuan per load for high-quality goods and 40 yuan for second-class goods. Yesterday, the company transported two packages of sample cocoons at the Gongchen Bridge Station on behalf of the customers, totaling more than 100 kilograms. One was purchased by the Xinyu Cocoon Firm in Yuhang and transported to the Jiucheng No. 2 Silk Factory in Shanghai, and the other was purchased by the Da'an Cocoon Firm in Hangyu Genshan Linping and other places and transported to the Tongyi Silk Factory in Shanghai. It is also reported that the whole batch of cocoon packages is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 15th and 16th of this month.

Spring cocoons produced in various parts of Zhejiang Province are now on the market, such as Gongchen, Yuhang, Linping, Xucun, and Chang'an. The official opening of the scales for purchase is scheduled for the 14th of this month. Therefore, silk factories and cocoon merchants in the Shanghai port have sent people to the above-mentioned places to set up purchases. The trip will depart from Shanghai at 7:00 a.m. today (the 10th). There are more than 300 silk merchant personnel, all taking the second Shanghai-Hangzhou Road early express train, and the Railway Bureau's Traffic Department has added four third-class passenger cars to the second passenger car for the cocoon merchants to take.

大樹椿重新建設 111

Reconstruction of Datshu Chuang

A Public Notice by the Customs Maritime Section Inspector Xi

This maritime inspection office is inspecting the reconstruction of the Datshu Chuang near the North Sea Port of Sha Xi Kou within the boundary of the Zhenjiang Customs. The situation is detailed below. The Datshu Chuang, near the North Sea Port of Sha Xi Kou in the Yangtze River, was reconstructed on May 2 of this year. The Chuang consists of a marker with a black round top and two unranked white constant lights. From the new location, the direction of the Duanshan Chuang is South 53 and 1/4 degrees East (according to the compass direction), and the distance is six and a half nautical miles. All nautical charts No. 12 published by the Maritime Affairs Bureau should be corrected accordingly. Therefore, all ships are hereby notified to pay close attention and record the details to avoid any mishaps. May 5, 19th year of the Republic of China.

Local News Two

九十歲老伶工 113

Ninety-Year-Old Opera Actor

孫菊仙訪問記

A Visit with Sun Juxian

天下人爲他做壽

The World Celebrates His Birthday

老鄕親張吻大笑

Elderly Compatriot Zhang Laughs Heartily

養生殊無獨得之秘

No Unique Secret to Maintaining Health

幼嗜武術長頑弓馬

Loved Martial Arts as a Child and Played with Bows and Arrows as an Adult

精神　鑠態度謙恭

Vigorous Spirit and Humble Demeanor

不日與滬人士相見

Will Meet with Shanghai People Soon

"I am old and no longer have the vigor of my youth. My coming to Shanghai this time is to escort the remains of my children to be buried in the Rainbow Bridge Township Cemetery. Speaking of which, it is inevitable to make people feel sad." Yesterday, the reporter visited Sun Juxian, the ninety-year-old opera actor known as "Elderly Compatriot," at the Yipinxiang Hotel and asked about his feelings on coming to Shanghai this time. He replied as above. The setting sun is fading, times have changed, and savoring the words of the "Elderly Compatriot," it seems impossible not to sigh with regret. Sun Juxian, from Tianjin, entered the opera world as a famous amateur and became a leader in the industry for sixty years. Empress Dowager Cixi of the late Qing Dynasty admired his art and selected him to be a court performer, living in the palace for eighteen years. Throughout his life, he was praised for his philanthropy and extraordinary spirit, different from the common customs. People respected him for his age and reputation, and dared not call him by his name. The three words "Elderly Compatriot" are a sign of respect. This time, he came to Shanghai to bury his descendants and will stay for a while. His friends invited him to share his unique artistry with the people of Shanghai, and thus there is a proposal for him to perform on the Shanghai stage. The reporter believes that it is a rare opportunity for this old man to come south. It is more than just an anecdote in the opera world for a nonagenarian to put on makeup and appear on stage. Therefore, the reporter went to visit him. The "Elderly Compatriot" is currently staying in room 15 of the Yipinxiang Hotel. He arrived in Shanghai on the 4th of this month by taking the Tongzhou wheel from Tianjin and arrived here at around 9:00 a.m. Those who knew Mr. Sun in the past went to chat with him. The reporter visited him last night at around 8:00 p.m. A fellow villager of his was talking to the "Elderly Compatriot" about matters since their separation. Although Mr. Sun is ninety years old, he does not show obvious signs of decline. He has a handful of white beard, both whiskers as white as frost, and looks like someone in his seventies. He wears a black robe and a coral-knotted casual hat. When entering the room, he bows with both hands, showing great respect. He holds a black pipe that is about three feet long and smokes a lot of tobacco after sitting down. When talking, his voice is loud and clear, coming from his dantian. However, he is deaf, and guests must speak loudly to him. The reporter exchanged pleasantries with him and asked about the purpose of his trip before proceeding with the following conversation.

(Question) How many times have you been to Shanghai before? (Answer) How many times? I can't remember anymore. I came to Shanghai sixty years ago when I was thirty years old and founded the Shengping Theater. Later, it closed due to heavy losses, so I returned north. This was my first time in Shanghai. (Question) It is extremely rare for the "Elderly Compatriot" to be ninety years old. Can you tell us your birth date? Upon hearing this, Sun Juxian suddenly opened his mouth and laughed at the reporter, saying, "I was born in the 21st year of the Daoguang Emperor of the former Qing Dynasty, isn't it ninety years ago? If you ask about my birthday, I don't need to remember it myself because the whole world celebrates my birthday!" At this point, he laughed even louder, seeming extremely happy in his heart. The reporter eagerly asked him for details. The "Elderly Compatriot" said, "To tell you the truth, my birthday is on the eve of the twelfth lunar month. Isn't it a time when candles are burning high, banquets are in full swing, and every family is celebrating the New Year, celebrating the birthday of this old man?" The reporter listened to his words and couldn't help but clap his hands in admiration, feeling that this old man still had the heart of a child and that it was indeed a sign of longevity. So, the reporter asked if he had any unique methods of maintaining health or any special ways to preserve youth. Mr. Sun replied, "I have no unique secret to maintaining health. However, I liked to practice martial arts when I was young, and as I grew older, I studied archery. I often exercised my muscles and bones. Perhaps that is why I am so healthy today." Later, the reporter chatted about trivial matters and then took his leave. The conversation lasted for about ten minutes, and the old man coughed only once or twice. His spirit was vigorous, and he did not deceive us.

娘子軍 114

Women's Army

大鬧民立中學

Causes Havoc at the Minli Middle School

蘇祖衍離婚妻尋釁

Su Zuyan's Divorced Wife Provokes Trouble

顧公量適首當其衝

Gu Gongliang Becomes the First Target

娘子軍實行總攻擊

The Women's Army Launches a Full Attack

中華路上觀者塞途

Spectators Jam the Streets of Zhonghua Road

Su Zuyan, a local teacher at Shanghai Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road, west of the South Gate in the Nanshi district, was divorced from his wife, Ms. Li, due to her fierceness and repeated abuse. He had filed a complaint with the local court last year, and a divorce was granted. The details were reported in this newspaper. However, Ms. Li was not satisfied and repeatedly provoked Mr. Su. Because Mr. Su was a professor and wanted to save face, he would avoid her whenever he heard that Ms. Li was coming. Ms. Li, angered and ashamed, searched for Mr. Su's address again and again. Almost all the officers in the 2nd Precinct of the Public Security Bureau recognized Ms. Li. After separating from Mr. Su, Ms. Li lived with relatives in No. 7 Zhilan Lane on Route Cardinal Foch in the French Concession, but she never forgot about Mr. Su. Yesterday at around 12:00 noon, Ms. Li and several female friends and neighbors hired a car from the Fuxing Automobile Company on Route Mareschal Joffre and drove directly to Minli Middle School. They rushed into the school, demanding that Mr. Su come out to talk. At that time, Mr. Gu Gongliang, a close friend of Mr. Su (also a teacher at Minli Middle School), heard the news and came out to stop Ms. Li from entering the school. However, when Ms. Li saw Mr. Gu, she became even more enraged. During the court hearing last year, Mr. Gu was the most powerful witness, testifying that he had personally seen Ms. Li slapping Mr. Su several times during a fight with his friends and that he had denounced Ms. Li as fierce and strongly advocated for a divorce. Therefore, Ms. Li hated Mr. Gu even more than an enemy. Before a word could be said, the women's army launched a full-scale attack, striking out with their hands and shouting insults. Mr. Gu Gongliang was helpless and was quickly beaten, suffering injuries to his head, back, and sides. For a time, the streets of Zhonghua Road were jammed with spectators, and more than ten trams were stopped. There were many students at Minli, and seeing their teacher being attacked, they wanted to come to his aid, but were afraid of causing a disaster because of gender relations. They had to report to the nearby police and send a telegram to the 2nd Precinct of the Public Security Bureau for help. Chief Meng heard the news and immediately ordered an inspector to lead several police officers to the scene. When they saw Ms. Li, whom they recognized instantly, they understood the situation without asking and took her and the car to the precinct. Chief Meng had just taken office and was meeting Ms. Li for the first time. He was about to ask for her age and address when a police officer replied, "She is 24 years old, a local, and used to live in Xinchengli nearby." He said it without thinking because Ms. Li had been brought to the precinct for fighting with Mr. Su more than once, so they were very familiar with her. The neighbors and friends who came with her were questioned. One identified herself as Ms. Li Xue, 40 years old, a local, living at No. 7 Zhilan Lane in the French Concession. Another identified herself as Ms. Liu Li, 42 years old, living with Ms. Li Xue and assisting in the crime. The driver identified himself as Wang Guixun, 27 years old, from Ningbo. Mr. Gu Gongliang, 26 years old, from Kunshan, gave a detailed account of Ms. Li's provocative behavior. After obtaining the statements, Chief Meng considered the matter to involve personal affairs and immediately prepared a document to transfer the case to the court for review.

市民銀行倒閉後 115

After the Collapse of the Citizen Bank

五萬兩控案

50,000 Taels Lawsuit

張維鏞吳希白在押

Zhang Weiyong and Wu Xibai in Custody

原告係向私人控追

Plaintiff Pursues Private Claims

註册問題大堪研究

Registration Issues Warrant Study

辯論終結定期宣判

Debate Concluded, Sentencing Scheduled

Since last winter, the China Citizen Bank, located at No. 19 Guangdong Road, has been repeatedly accused of fraud, causing its reputation and credit to decline. However, it勉力 supported itself until a few days ago when Zhang Weiyong, the managing director in charge of the bank's affairs, and Wu Xibai, the general manager, were sued by Lü Ziqing, and the Special District Court detained them, leading to the suspension of business. Lü, from Ningbo, is currently a comprador for Dadah Foreign Firm. In March, Lü hired lawyer Ye Fukang to sue Zhang Weiyong, Wu Xibai, and guarantor La Wenyuan in the Former Provisional Court for failing to repay 50,000 taels of silver in two loans.

The first loan was for 20,000 taels. According to the indictment, in July of last year, Wu exchanged three China Citizen Bank cashier's checks for 15,000 taels of cash from Lü. When the checks were due, he failed to pay the money. After Lü repeatedly demanded payment, Wu finally pledged his own 20,000 tael shares in the bank and a property deed and sales contract for a plot of land in Shangyi, Bao 25, under the name of Cao Jixun, as collateral on October 16th. He also had La Wenyuan guarantee the loan of 20,000 taels, and a contract was signed with a redemption date of December 31st.

The second loan was for 30,000 taels. On December 1st, Wu told Lü that to maintain the bank's business, he needed to borrow another 30,000 taels. Otherwise, the bank would not be able to operate and would have to close down, and the previous loan of 20,000 taels would also be lost. Lü had to agree to his request. Wu and Zhang, representing the bank, jointly signed a document stating that the bank's business rights, property rights, registration certificate, and all its movable and immovable property would be used as collateral, also with a redemption date at the end of the year. However, at the due date, no money was repaid.

Separate Lawsuits for Repayment. After Lü's investigation, apart from a valid land deed under the name of Cao Ji Dong, the other collateral was worthless. Therefore, he filed a lawsuit. For the first loan of 20,000 taels, he requested the court to order Wu Xibai to repay the money and hold the guarantor La Wenyuan jointly and severally liable. For the second loan of 30,000 taels, he requested the court to order Wu Xibai and Zhang Weiyong to jointly repay the money.

Wu and Zhang Arrested and Detained. They also declared that Wu and Zhang were at risk of fleeing. The plaintiff was willing to provide 20,000 taels of cash as bail and requested that the two defendants be arrested and detained. As a result, Zhang Weiyong and Wu Xibai, who had both served as chairmen of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, were detained. The bank initially continued to operate until it was unable to sustain itself and declared liquidation a few days ago.

The Plaintiff Was Once the Bank's President. Yesterday morning, the case was heard by Judge Xu Wenrong of the Special District Court. The three defendants each hired lawyers to defend them. The plaintiff first stated the circumstances of the two loans, presented the loan documents and letters as evidence, and denied holding the position of president of the bank. According to the testimony of defendant Zhang Weiyong, the plaintiff denied holding the position of president after taking office because he could not implement his plans for personal gain. However, all the important keys to the bank were still in his hands, and two of his close associates only resigned when the lawsuit was about to be filed. While he was president, depositors who tried to withdraw money were not only denied payment but also insulted. He is currently being sued in the French Concession, and so on. He also presented the bank's business books and delivery books signed by the plaintiff to prove that Lü was indeed the president of the bank.

Fraudulent Registration to Deceive. The debate began. First, lawyer Ye stated that the bank was established before raising funds and claimed to be registered with the Hong Kong government. However, according to the British Companies Act passed by the British Parliament after 1928, it must be registered with the local consulate to be recognized as a British company. The bank did not register with the British Consulate in Shanghai and was actually fraudulently deceiving people.

Wu Should Repay 20,000 Taels. If the plaintiff was indeed the president, there should be letters of appointment, etc. The delivery book is not sufficient evidence. His signature on the bank's business books is because the loan document states that the business rights are also within the scope of the collateral. The defendants specifically invited Lü to the bank and colluded with people to deposit a small amount of money to make Lü sign, to strengthen his belief that the bank did indeed have depositors and to use it as bait to borrow money. The wording of the 20,000 tael loan clearly indicates that it was Wu's personal loan, so Wu should repay it, and La should bear the responsibility of guarantee. The 30,000 tael loan should be jointly repaid by Wu and Zhang, and overdue interest should be paid.

The Question of the President's Responsibility. The defendants' lawyers then argued, first stating that the amount of the loan did not match, indicating that there was an inside story. Next, they discussed the issue of responsibility and requested that the plaintiff was actually the president of the bank and that all the bank's accounts were stored in the vault, with the keys still in the plaintiff's possession. They requested that he hand them over so that the books could be retrieved for investigation, which would clarify the exact amount of the loan and its use.

Agreed to Consulate Investigation. They also agreed with the plaintiff's lawyer's request to investigate with the British Consulate, saying that this would not only resolve the dispute over whether it was registered with the British Consulate but also prove whether the plaintiff was a shareholder of the bank.

The Debate Was Declared Concluded. After the debate, the defendants' lawyers raised two more points: (1) Zhang and Wu have been detained for two months, causing great losses to the bank, leading to its closure. The right to claim damages should be reserved. (2) Please release the defendants. Judge Xu ruled that the debate on the case was concluded and that the sentencing would be scheduled for the morning of May 12. The defendants Zhang Weiyong and Wu Xibai were returned to custody and ordered to provide bail pending approval for release on bail.

特區法院開審 116

The Special District Court Opens Trial

六十萬大騙案

600,000 Dollar Fraud Case

最初放印子錢於妓寮

Initially Loaned Money at High Interest to Brothels

貪厚息存户逐漸增多

Depositors Gradually Increased Due to Greed for High Interest

付息金多至四十六萬

Interest Payments Reached 460,000

法院淸理被告之財產

The Court Liquidates the Defendant's Assets

Yang Shulin, a native of Hebei who previously served as a patrol officer in the Fourth District Police Department in Zhabei, falsely established a company in the name of running a real business after resigning from his public service position, defrauding people of a huge amount of 600,000 dollars in deposits. The case has been reported in this newspaper. The cause of this massive fraud was due in part to those who were greedy for high interest rates.

Delivering Interest House to House. Yang initially started by lending money at high interest, mostly to brothels on Sima Road, to be used as basic capital for the prostitution business, charging a monthly interest rate of six cents. As the number of borrowers increased, Yang's capital became limited. Therefore, he had a whimsical idea and re-lent the money to others, luring them with high interest rates, giving them five cents per month. At the time of interest payments, he sent people to deliver the money house to house. As a result, greedy and contemptible people, blinded by greed, successively deposited money with him, eventually losing both principal and interest. Although some had received a little interest money, it was still not worth the loss.

Complex Depositor Base. There are a total of one thousand depositors, with a complex mix of educated people, government employees, businessmen, women, and male and female laborers. They have now formed a creditors' group, initially handled by lawyer Ye Fukang. However, only a few people registered with Ye. Later, it was changed to be handled by lawyers Xu Bingcheng and Xu Fuji, father and son. More than 390 people have registered with Xu.

Deposits Accumulated More and More. Xu was originally the legal advisor of the Wenji Company established by Yang and is now representing the creditors of the company and filing a lawsuit on behalf of the creditors. The complaint describes in detail that the defendant Yang Shulin founded the Hexing Company in the Bingyin year, established the Wenji Company in the Dingmao year, and then successively established more than a dozen branches. Seeing the increasing number of branches and the expansion of business, the old depositors, in addition to receiving official interest, also received bonuses. As a result, the news spread, and more and more people believed in him, and the deposits increased more and more.

His Concubine is Still at Large. After Yang falsely claimed to have been kidnapped on February 14 of this year, the creditors initially believed it to be true and publicly elected Gu Zhuxuan and Cao Youshan to try to maintain the situation. At this time, it was discovered that the deposits of each household reached more than 600,000. While registering and liquidating, they suddenly received news that Yang Cunyang had been detained in Tianjin. The depositors realized that Yang had malicious intentions. Cao sent someone to Tianjin to accompany him back to Shanghai to try to remedy the situation. Unexpectedly, after returning to Shanghai, he kept delaying and fabricating accounts. On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, Yang and his concubine Chen Huanxi were about to flee together. Fortunately, He Qiqing was captured first. After he revealed the hiding place, Yang was subsequently arrested, but his concubine is still at large.

Requesting Strict Arrest of Yang's Concubine. The money Yang defrauded was mostly from the autumn and winter seasons of last year, amounting to 360,000 to 370,000. When he was detained in Tianjin, his concubine revealed the truth, saying that the kidnapping was a lie and that she had moved the suitcases to hide them. Therefore, Yang's concubine was actually colluding with him. It is requested that she be strictly arrested and brought to justice.

The Falsely Claimed Kidnapping Money Should Be Recovered. Also, Yang sent two letters from Tianjin, saying that he was carrying 52,000 dollars in cash when he was kidnapped. Now that the kidnapping claim has been proven to be false, Yang should be ordered to hand over the money.

The Bad Debts Are Obviously Fabricated. Also, in the business statement made by Yang, the third item shows 51,290 dollars in bad debts from Bingyin to Gengwu. However, after searching the account books, there is no such record. It is obviously fabricated and should also be ordered to be handed over by Yang first. There are many other inconsistencies in the accounts. It is requested that a detailed investigation be conducted before severely punishing Yang.

The Branches Have No Scale. The statement mentions that there are more than a dozen branches, referring to the Wenji Bee Company, the Prida Steel Factory, the Health Vegetable

Page 16

Garden, the Hexing Money Shop, the Hexing Gold Shop, the Heshengyong, the Hesheng, etc., in addition to the Hexing and Wenji Companies. However, after examining the reality, it is truly laughable. The so-called steel factory is actually an iron shop, and the health vegetable garden is a rented piece of land in a remote area of Zhabei, used as a vegetable garden to grow and sell vegetables. As for the Hexing Gold Shop and the Hexing Money Shop, the capital is very small. The others are not worth mentioning.

More Than 300 People Arrived in Court. Yesterday afternoon, the case was heard by Judge Sun Yuan of the Special District Court in the Third Courtroom. The two defendants, Yang Shulin and He Qiqing, were ordered to be brought before the court for interrogation. No less than 300 male and female creditors arrived, and their litigation representatives were Cao Youshan, Ge Qingshan, Zhu Shuo, Zheng Qiongji, Shi Youhui, Zhu Qishi, Dong Zhihe, Lu Yushan, Yang Haigen, Wang Zhongji, Shang Decheng, Liu Ziying, and 12 others. First, the 12 people stated the amount of their deposits, and some presented deposit receipts. This deposit was neither a deposit book nor a deposit slip, and its form was similar to a loan document.

Yang Shulin's Testimony. According to the interrogation of defendant Yang Shulin by Judge Sun, Wenji was opened in the seventh year and initially only loaned money at high interest, charging six cents. It was not until the twelfth year that it began to absorb deposits and give five cents interest. Most of the depositors were introduced by friends. By the fifteenth year, there were more and more depositors. In the seventeenth year, the government issued an order prohibiting the exploitation of high interest, and I planned to change my ways and started a real business. At the end of last year, I was unable to pay the five cents interest and changed it to three cents. The depositors then rushed to withdraw their money, and it was impossible to maintain the situation. I had to falsely claim to have been kidnapped and fled to Tianjin. But I have no property in my hometown. All the interest I paid to the depositors has receipts that can be checked.

460,000 in Interest Payments. He then described the locations of each branch and the amount of capital and the name of the manager in each place. He said that the total capital of its branches was less than 50,000. Most of the managers were idle people from the police force. Judge Sun sternly questioned him about how he used such a huge amount of money. Yang then claimed that the amount of money released was about 320,000, and the amount of interest paid was more than 460,000, all of which could be checked in the accounts.

The Runner is Still Confused. He Qiqing was then interrogated. According to his testimony, he worked as a runner for the Hexing Company. Hexing specialized in discounted bills of exchange, and Wenji Company was engaged in lending money at high interest. He is an illiterate fool and seems to be unaware of Yang's fraudulent behavior. He firmly claimed that the discounted bills of exchange he released could be collected from the issuer. He still did not know that Yang had already collected the bills from the issuer after they were due. After a long interrogation, Judge Sun ordered the two defendants to be returned to custody for further investigation and decided to have the court appoint someone to be responsible for the liquidation of the defendant's property because it was an important matter.

Public Opposition to Takahashi Sands 117

Sale of Shatin to Foreign Merchants

Texaco's Land Purchase for Oil Tank Construction Sparks Repercussions

Jiang Ruchun, manager of Yongxing Real Estate Company, bought more than 200 mu of Shatin land at Takahashi Sands (i.e., Mouse Sands) and sold it to the foreign merchant Texaco for the purpose of building oil tanks. The residents of Shatin believe that Jiang Ruchun disregards the people's livelihood, is greedy for huge profits, calls it a lease, but it is actually a bill of sale, selling off national territory, benefiting himself and harming the people. Nothing could be worse. They specially gathered two or three hundred residents a few days ago to hold a meeting at Shatin. Lu Wenbiao, Xu Yunlong, Huang Wenxiang, Zhong Youliang, Gu Quan, and others were publicly elected as representatives. They should, according to law, sue the national government to severely investigate the lawless and treacherous villains and confiscate the land, striving to achieve the goal. Six Sons-in-Law One After Another 120

How Many Husbands Can One Woman Marry?

The Inside Story of Divorce

In Hongjialong, West City, Sanlintang, Pudong, there is a Hong Guixiang, who is a shoemaker. His family is well-off, and he has only two daughters. The elder one is married and lives with her husband's family. The younger daughter, nicknamed Guifan, is now twenty years old. Three years ago, he recruited Lu Bingquan to his home as his son-in-law, originally planning to get married in July this year. Now Hong Guifan believes that her fiancé Lu Bingquan does not obey her father's teachings and is dissatisfied. She asked someone to write a petition to the local court, requesting to terminate the engagement. The defendant, Lu Bingquan, hired lawyer Zhang Qingyue to file a defense. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, Judge Zhao Zhenhai specially opened the second court for trial. First, the plaintiff Hong Guifan testified, "I am twenty years old, from Shanghai, and live in Hongjialong, Sanlintang, Pudong." (Question) "What are you requesting?" (Answer) "Request to terminate the engagement." (Question) "When did you get engaged?" (Answer) "About five or six years ago." (Question) "Who made the decision?" (Answer) "My parents made the decision." (Question) "Who was the matchmaker?" (Answer) "Someone surnamed Cai." (Question) "Did your parents ask you when you got engaged?" (Answer) "No." (Question) "How many years has Lu Bingquan been in your house?" (Answer) "Three years." At this point, lawyer Zhang spoke up, "The engagement was made on the tenth day of the first month of the lunar calendar in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China. At that time, the defendant Lu Bingquan came to the door, commonly known as a 'male daughter-in-law.' Please pay attention to the plaintiff's age, Your Honor. Although she is nominally twenty years old this year, she is actually only nineteen years old and has not reached the legal age." The judge then (asked) "When is the plaintiff's birthday?" Guifan (replied) "I was born on the twenty-fifth day of the first month." The judge said, "Then you are indeed not yet twenty years old. It must be postponed until the twenty-fifth day of the first month next year to be legal." (Answer) "In our village, we count one year older after the new year." (Question) "Does your father know about this lawsuit?" (Answer) "Yes." (Question) "Since you didn't want to, why didn't you object at the time?" (Answer) "I didn't know his personality at the time. After he came to the door, my father taught him how to make a living (referring to making shoes), but he refused to do it and ran away, and said that he didn't want me to be his wife." (Question) "Was there any evidence when Lu Bingquan came to the door?" ( ) "Yes, it's at my father's place." The judge ordered Lu Bingquan to the case to testify. He is twenty years old, from Shanghai, lives in Sanlintang, and is now a partner in Jiang Wansheng Rice Store in Xieqiao. (Question) "The plaintiff is requesting to terminate the engagement. What do you think?" (Answer) "I don't want to. I must have her." (Question) "Who made the decision in your family when you got engaged?" (Answer) "My elder brother Jinquan made the decision." (Question) "What about the woman's family?" (Answer) "My father-in-law and mother-in-law made the decision." (Question) "Are you and her on good terms?" (Answer) "Yes." (Question) "Is it true that you don't listen to her father's words?" (Answer) "I listen." (Question) "Why doesn't she want you?" (Answer) "They beat me out." (Question) "Why doesn't your father-in-law like you?" (Answer) "Because I don't make shoes with my father-in-law, so he doesn't like me. But everyone has their own ambitions. I want to work in the rice industry. Besides, I used to learn the trade at Suilong Rice Store, and my monthly salary was eight yuan. Because it was not enough to cover expenses, I have now been transferred to Jiang Wansheng Rice Store in Xieqiao as a partner, with a monthly salary of fourteen yuan," etc. According to Hong Guixiang's testimony, she is fifty-one years old. "When I betrothed my daughter Guifan in the past, she was only sixteen years old. I have tried to persuade my daughter about this lawsuit, but she refused." (Question) "What's wrong with Lu Bingquan?" (Answer) "He used to learn at a rice store. After he came to the door, I taught him to make shoes, but he didn't listen to me and ran away." (Question) "How much money can you earn each month making shoes?" (Answer) "About twenty yuan." The judge said, "Now the court orders the defendant to make shoes with you and listen to you. How about that?" (Answer) "His personality is inherent, how can it be changed?" Then the judge said to the defendant, "How about you still make shoes with your father-in-law?" (Answer) "I have hope in the rice industry. If I go to make shoes, there is no future. I cannot agree." At this point, lawyer Zhang said, "Since the defendant came to the door, he has been deceived by the plaintiff's father out of 210 yuan and a gold ring. Now the defendant has no money, so the plaintiff doesn't want the defendant. However, there is a dark side to this kind of recruiting a son-in-law. There have been as many as six fiancés recruited by the plaintiff, including the defendant. It is worth studying." Lawyer Zhang then presented a list of the plaintiff's previous fiancés to the case for review. (1. Yao Sheng, son of Gao Qiutang; 2. Qiu Jian, son of Wang Gengsheng; 3. Nephew of Zhang Arong, name unknown; 4. Grand-nephew of Qu Muquan, name unknown; 5. Xue Yu, son of Qiao Xuelin.) After reading it, the judge asked Hong, "Is this true?" (Answer) "Yes, there are only two sons of Gao Qiutang. Because there are adopted sons and apprentices, they all refer to them as my son-in-law, which is too much." The defendant said, "There are actually six people. Yao Sheng, son of Gao Qiutang, was in the eighth year of the Republic of China; Qiu Jian, son of Wang Gengsheng, was in the tenth year of the Republic of China; Zhang Arong's nephew was in the eleventh year of the Republic of China; Qu Muquan's grand-nephew was in the twelfth year of the Republic of China; Xue Yu, son of Qiao Xuelin, was in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China; I was in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China." The judge obtained the testimony and mediated on the spot, persuading the plaintiff to withdraw the lawsuit. The plaintiff refused and insisted on terminating the engagement. The judge said, "Words cannot be spoken casually. Besides, you are betrothed to too many people, and the reputation is not good." Lawyer Zhang also said, "The defendant was originally scheduled to get married in July this year, and now there is a seventh person behind the scenes, so there is this lawsuit," etc. The judge learned the truth and said to Hong Guifan, "If you want to terminate the engagement, you must compensate the defendant 210 yuan, otherwise, there is only a judgment according to law." The plaintiff replied that she had no money. The judge ordered that there would be no debate, and ordered both parties to go outside for mediation. If the mediation failed, they would convene again for trial, and then adjourned the court.

The Price of a Wife 121

Transferred for 160 Yuan

Mother-in-Law Learns of it and is Infuriated

Xiao Meimei, the daughter of Feng Xie, a woman in Xintou Lane, Northwest Shanghai, is 26 years old this year. Four years ago, she married Yan Xiaodi, a farmer. Yan has a scabby head and an extremely ugly appearance. The relationship between the couple is like ice and charcoal, and they often fight. In April last year, the couple quarreled again. Xiao Meimei left in a fit of anger. When she arrived at Xujiahui, it was already dusk and there was nowhere to stay. Ai Bingkui, a farmer from Aijiazhai there, struck up a conversation. Because his parents were both dead and he had no wife, this unexpected encounter was a match made in heaven. He led her home and they engaged in illicit relations. From then on, Xiao Meimei was in charge of the Ai family's cooking and housekeeping. Soon, the news spread, and Yan Xiaodi learned about it. He went to the Ai family to negotiate. Ai's aunt, Jin, and Ai negotiated with Yan to pay 160 yuan as the price for the body. Yan Xiaodi agreed and wrote a document transferring his wife. After Yan Xiaodi got 160 yuan and returned home, he had used it all up in a year. He had no more money, and because his mother-in-law Feng Xie had not yet known about it, he could not bear the burden if the secret was leaked. So, as a preemptive measure, he often went to Feng Xie's place to inquire about his wife's whereabouts. The woman originally thought that her daughter had really escaped, so she agreed to ask someone to look for her. Later, she was reported that Yan Xiaodi had sold his wife himself. The woman was furious and rushed to Yan's house the day before yesterday, taking Yan to the Sixth District First Sub-bureau. A senior police officer was then dispatched to bring Ai Bingkui and Jin Ai to the station. Yesterday, together with the plaintiff, they were transferred to the local court for interrogation.

Japanese 122

Will Auction Luggage of Detained Chinese

Since Japan strictly prohibits Chinese laborers from going to Japan, how many thousands of people have been deported back to Shanghai in the past? Hankou Road 123

One-Way Traffic Temporarily Postponed

Regulations to be Determined After Three Months

All the shops on Hankou Road previously stated that the implementation of one-way traffic had greatly affected business. They had sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce and the Taxpaying Chinese Association to request its cancellation. It is now learned that the Chamber of Commerce received a reply from the Public Works Department yesterday, which stated: "The Bureau's intention in taking this measure is purely for the public interest. The Bureau's view is that the interests of a few people, no matter who these few people are, can never outweigh the interests of the general public. Therefore, although the merchants on Hankou Road may feel inconvenience, the Bureau has a compassionate heart and is unwilling to cancel this one-way traffic regulation. It should be implemented as usual within the stipulated three months (starting from April 1). After the three months expire, the Bureau will then determine whether the one-way traffic method on Hankou Road should be continued based on the advantages and disadvantages seen during this trial period. As for the alleged inconvenience felt by merchants, I believe that if given time and implemented for a long time, this inconvenience will gradually decrease. As this regulation has been known to the public, it will surely enable those who drive on this road to go to their destination from the appropriate direction. In all major cities, the one-way traffic method and the "no right turn" regulation are becoming increasingly necessary. This is because the traffic of vehicles is increasing day by day, and this is not enough to manage their actions and facilitate their travel. Assuming that the restrictions of the rules are enough to cause inconvenience to pedestrians and operators in this location, they guarantee the safety of the majority, increase the convenience of the majority, and promote the smooth and unobstructed traffic of the entire street market. Comparing the advantages and disadvantages, the importance cannot be discussed on the same day. In these major cities, it is almost impossible for pedestrians to go to a place in the commercial area and want to reach the door directly by vehicle, and vehicles often park far away and must get out of the car to walk, it is said.
